      {
        "inputs": [
          {
            "internalType": "address",
            "name": "account",

          },
          {
            "internalType": "uint256",
            "name": "id",
            "type": "uint256"
          }
        ],
        "name": "balanceOf",
        "outputs": [
          {
            "internalType": "uint256",
            "name": "",
            "type": "uint256"
          }

        "type": "function"
      },
